 interface StoryState {
+  staticRoutes: RouteData[];
+  modRoutes: RouteData[];
   storyJSON: StoryJSON;
   currentRouteId: string | null;
   
   // Actions
   setRoute: (routeId: string) => void;
+  setModRoutes: (routes: RouteData[]) => void;
   getRoute: (routeId: string) => RouteData | undefined;

+const computeStoryJSON = (staticRoutes: RouteData[], modRoutes: RouteData[]): StoryJSON => {
+  const routeMap = new Map<string, RouteData>();
+  
+  // Add static routes first
+  staticRoutes.forEach(r => routeMap.set(r.id, r));
+  
+  // Add mod routes with Namespace isolation to prevent ID conflicts
+  modRoutes.forEach(r => {
+    const modId = r.modId || 'unknown_mod';
+    // Local workspace routes keep their original ID to prevent breaking existing saves
+    // Downloaded mods get namespaced
+    const isLocalWorkspace = modId === 'local_workspace';
+    const namespacedId = isLocalWorkspace ? r.id : `${modId}__${r.id}`;
+    
+    const namespacedRoute = { ...r, id: namespacedId };
+    
+    // Add UI distinguish mark for downloaded mods if not present
+    if (!isLocalWorkspace && !namespacedRoute.title.endsWith('[Mod]')) {
+      namespacedRoute.title = `${namespacedRoute.title} [Mod]`;
+    }
+    
+    routeMap.set(namespacedRoute.id, namespacedRoute);
+  });
+  
+  return { routes: Array.from(routeMap.values()) };
+};
+

+/**
+ * 鎻愬彇鐩爣鍑芥暟涓殑鎵€鏈夋湭鐭ユ暟锛堥櫎 x 鍜?y 澶栵級锛岃繑鍥炰竴涓柊鐨勫弬鏁板瓧鍏?+ * 瀵逛簬鐜版湁鐨勫弬鏁颁繚鐣欏叾鍊硷紝鏂扮殑鍙傛暟榛樿璧嬪€间负 1
+ */
+export function autoExtractParams(latex: string, currentParams: Record<string, number> | null | undefined): Record<string, number> | null {
+  if (!latex) return currentParams || null;
+  try {
+    const cleanLatex = cleanDesmosLatex(latex);
+    const box = ce.parse(cleanLatex);
+    const simplifiedBox = box.simplify();
+    const unknowns = simplifiedBox.unknowns || [];
+    
+    const newParams: Record<string, number> = {};
+    let hasParams = false;
+
+    for (const v of unknowns) {
+      if (v !== 'x' && v !== 'y') {
+        hasParams = true;
+        // 淇濈暀鍘熸湁鐨勫€硷紝濡傛灉鏄柊鍙傛暟鍒欓粯璁よ祴鍊间负 1
+        newParams[v] = (currentParams && v in currentParams) ? currentParams[v] : 1;
+      }
+    }
+
+    return hasParams ? newParams : null;
+  } catch (error) {
+    logger.error(SYSTEM_LOGS.MATH_PARSE_PARAM_ERROR, error);
+    return currentParams || null;
+  }
+}
